<div id="review_358396242" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/358396242" />
    <a title="Between the Bind" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4549101-between-the-bind"><img alt="Between the Bind" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1341769009p2/4549101.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/358396242?book_show_action=true">Jun 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Between the Bind" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Between the Bind" href="/user/show/4549101-between-the-bind">Between the Bind</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer358396242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15205480826507856276">Full review: <a href='http://betweenthebind.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Between the Bind</a><br/><br/>Firstly, look at that amazing cover?! Just captivating. I love having a visual of the "Cat's Eye" on this cover. And although Sora has golden blonde hair, the strawberry tint is very attractive. Now to the gushy! <br/><br/>Ms. Shreffler is making Sora's Quest FREE for 72 hours after this is posted (July 9-11) - so hurry and nab your free copy HERE! *high five* If you'd like, please thank her in a comment below. :)<br/><br/><u>Sum it up</u>:<br/>Sora, tired of her simple and boring girl-in-the-manor</span>
  <span id="freeText15205480826507856276" style="display:none">Full review: <a href="http://betweenthebind.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Between the Bind</a><br /><br />Firstly, look at that amazing cover?! Just captivating. I love having a visual of the "Cat's Eye" on this cover. And although Sora has golden blonde hair, the strawberry tint is very attractive. Now to the gushy! <br /><br />Ms. Shreffler is making Sora's Quest FREE for 72 hours after this is posted (July 9-11) - so hurry and nab your free copy HERE! *high five* If you'd like, please thank her in a comment below. :)<br /><br /><u>Sum it up</u>:<br />Sora, tired of her simple and boring girl-in-the-manor life, plans to escape the night of her wedding, wanting nothing more than adventures like the "stories of old." She has no idea that her desire will be fulfilled via a kidnapping - by the very assassin who murdered her father, giving her the very opening to escape, and his two Wolfy companions. What begins as hatred, turns to timid trust and wary friendship between Sora and her captors.<br /><br /><u>The yum</u>:<br />Crash, the assassin, is mysterious up until the last page in Sora's Quest. Sexy, scary, and quiet are the three words best used to describe the man who seems to be running from his past. Ms. Shreffler has an interesting way of making her characters super sexy without being overt about their physical prowess or bragging about their beautiful features. Crash just is. Yum! ;)<br /><br />Dorian, a mage Wolfy, is an effeminate creature with a biting sarcastic and endearing quality about him. I liked Dorian immediately - especially because he called Sora out on her irritating princessy qualities.<br /><br />Burn is a large burly mercenary Wolfy that I just wanted to squeeze. He is the most open and kind of the three but still hosts his own unexplored demons.<br /><br /><u>Romance</u>?<br />There was plenty of awareness occurring in Sora's Quest and I was waiting for a romance to unfold - but it seems like I have to wait until Viper's Creed (Book 2) to *hopefully* see some woo-age occur.<br /><br /><u>Overall</u>:<br />Sora was a typical teenager and certainly irritated me throughout the book, but looking back, I love how the voice of Sora's voice ages from beginning to end.<br /><br />The antagonist was a clever one, coming up with evil and interesting ways to follow, capture, and manipulate his prey. I enjoyed Volcrian, and the sympathy the reader had for him from chapter one.<br /><br />So why the missing star, you ask? There were a LOT of unanswered questions: Who is Crash? Why are Crash, Burn, and Dorian together? Why did Crash murder Volcrian's twin and Sora's dad? What is a "protector" and is that what Crash is to Sora? <br /><br />After the entire book, I still am confused about our main characters. But I managed to really connect to them too.<br /><br />I can't WAIT until Book 2 - released in winter of 2012. Grab your copy and tell me what you think! :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="15205480826507856276" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1445648545" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1445648545" />
    <a title="Pallabi Dutta" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40136313-pallabi-dutta"><img alt="Pallabi Dutta" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555611504p2/40136313.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1445648545?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pallabi Dutta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pallabi Dutta" href="/user/show/40136313-pallabi-dutta">Pallabi Dutta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1445648545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17182626582150254952">4 stars.<br/>So this book is permanently free on amazon, so I thought why not? I downloaded it on kindle. It was everything I was hoping for. <br/>Sora, the protagonist of the story wants to lead a life of adventure, to live freely but her Lord Father and society expects her to marry on her seventeen birthday, when a blooming ceremony is held and suitors come forward but Sora has other plans. She plots to run away after the ceremony ends, to search for her mother but things don't go as planned. Abruptly s</span>
  <span id="freeText17182626582150254952" style="display:none">4 stars.<br />So this book is permanently free on amazon, so I thought why not? I downloaded it on kindle. It was everything I was hoping for. <br />Sora, the protagonist of the story wants to lead a life of adventure, to live freely but her Lord Father and society expects her to marry on her seventeen birthday, when a blooming ceremony is held and suitors come forward but Sora has other plans. She plots to run away after the ceremony ends, to search for her mother but things don't go as planned. Abruptly something happens at the ceremony and chaos ensues. She is at the wrong place at the wrong time, she was running away but in turn is actually kidnapped by a Assassin. Thus her adventure starts. She is stuck with the Assassin- Crash and his companion Dorian and Burn- a Wulven or Wolfie; an ancient race of magical beings, last of their kind. At the blooming ceremony, her father is killed and everybody thinks she killed her Lord father. The Crown is after her, she is kidnapped and made to journey with the assassin, the thief and the mercenary against her will. After certain misadventures she has no where to go but with them. And to top it all Volcrian- a Wulven mage is hunting the assassin for revenge for killing his brother. And only one thing stands between Volcrian and Crash and that is Sora and her Cat's eye necklace which protects it's wearer from magical attacks.<br />And Thank god, there is no insta love or love triangle. And the characters were complex to read and understand because when you think about it, all Volcrian is trying to do is get revenge on Crash for killing his brother but here he is the villain. And Crash or Viper(his real name) is an assassin and kills for money. Nobody is innocent or good, just circumstances are making them villain and hero out of them. <br />And Sora is in the middle of it all. Crash wouldn't let her go because she is the key which will help him keep alive. We see Sora at the start as a naive little girl but she grows well. She takes everything in stride. It's a fun read where there is little or no romance but adventure and action. The world building is something which was lacking a little but the writing was beautiful. We are left with a bitter sweet ending. I can't wait to read the second book in the series.<br />I loved reading this book and finished it in just one sitting. Recommended to everybody. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17182626582150254952" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_439228942" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/439228942" />
    <a title="Michelle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4253940-michelle"><img alt="Michelle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428021060p2/4253940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/439228942?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle " href="/user/show/4253940-michelle">Michelle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4253940-michelle?shelf=review-on-blog">review-on-blog</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4253940-michelle?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer439228942" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11319077330068899827">I have to be honest, after reading the first few chapters of the book, I didn't think I was going to like it too much. Now thinking about it, that was way too early for me to even be thinking about writing off any book, let alone a review book. So I kept on reading, and from the moment Sora left the castle, I was riveted! I ended up enjoying Sora's Quest so much. It just had a bit of a slow start to me and then it really took off. The part I didn't enjoy at the beginning seems like only one spec</span>
  <span id="freeText11319077330068899827" style="display:none">I have to be honest, after reading the first few chapters of the book, I didn't think I was going to like it too much. Now thinking about it, that was way too early for me to even be thinking about writing off any book, let alone a review book. So I kept on reading, and from the moment Sora left the castle, I was riveted! I ended up enjoying Sora's Quest so much. It just had a bit of a slow start to me and then it really took off. The part I didn't enjoy at the beginning seems like only one speck of the story- and Sora's Quest is a great story. <br /><br />Sora seems like a pretty sheltered girl at first but she certainly can rise to an occasion. This must have been so scary for her, being out in the world for the first time. It seemed a little crazy that she was so close to the guys in her group so fast considering the circumstances but her being so excited about being out in the world and the whole idea of an adventure didn't make her actions and emotions seem out of place. It kinda worked well. <br /><br />The world building is the best part! I loved learning all about the different people and the magics. T.L. Shreffler does a great job of explaining everything. I would have liked to see a little bit more back story on Crash. I didn't really know what they were doing at the start of the book except that they were on the run from Volcrian. But I think that is coming in the next book, so I look forward to getting some answers. I really enjoyed the character growth I saw in Crash throughout the story. The whole fear thing was super cute! (you will know exactly what I mean when you read the story) Fans of fantasy will love the world created in T.L. Shreffler's first installment in the Cat's Eye series. The ending made me want to drop everything and start book 2 right then!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11319077330068899827" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_366637656" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/366637656" />
    <a title="Victoria" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9890884-victoria"><img alt="Victoria" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338409623p2/9890884.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/366637656?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Victoria" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Victoria" href="/user/show/9890884-victoria">Victoria</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer366637656" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7023713723168814294">I'm going to rant here for a moment; Why go through the effort of writing a good piece of work and then fail to have a good editor? Perhaps no editor at all? I get the fact that spell check will not catch a word that is out of context but a good editor should. At the least get a friend to read your work, heck I'd do it for free. There is nothing more disconcerting than seeing fowl used for foul or effect for affect, unfortunately this seems to be on the rise with the popularity of ebooks. End ra</span>
  <span id="freeText7023713723168814294" style="display:none">I'm going to rant here for a moment; Why go through the effort of writing a good piece of work and then fail to have a good editor? Perhaps no editor at all? I get the fact that spell check will not catch a word that is out of context but a good editor should. At the least get a friend to read your work, heck I'd do it for free. There is nothing more disconcerting than seeing fowl used for foul or effect for affect, unfortunately this seems to be on the rise with the popularity of ebooks. End rant.<br /><br />Loved the story. I was expecting it to be a YA novel due to the cover art but I was pleasantly surprised to find a well written tale and likeable characters I think will appeal to both YA and adults equally. Sora plots to run away only hours before her unwelcome wedding only to be kidnapped(for no real apparent reason). She then finds herself teamed up with an unlikely band of Wolfy thieves and a cold assassin on the run from a dark mage.(to no place specific and towards no real goal) <br /><br />There is a slight lack of a well thought out plot, which coupled with the editing errors garnered this book only 3 stars out of 4. Hopefully book 2, due out in September, will give a little more purpose to our characters. I look forward to reading more of this world!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7023713723168814294" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1090222173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14833564866686383696"><b>I DID NOT EXPECT THIS!</b><br/><br/>This is such an amazing book! The essence of Fantasy done right! <br/><br/>When I started the book, I had a stomach flop moment where i was like <i>"Oh dear, rich girl hating her privileged life...great"</i> but Shreffler made me eat my words and for the first time <u>I didn't mind whatsoever!</u><br/><br/>Sora is an amazing character! She is not an amazingly strong girl, but she has spunk! The right amount of spunk that made you love her as the book progressed. <br/><br/>Shreffler made me adore ALL the characters, t</span>
  <span id="freeText14833564866686383696" style="display:none"><b>I DID NOT EXPECT THIS!</b><br /><br />This is such an amazing book! The essence of Fantasy done right! <br /><br />When I started the book, I had a stomach flop moment where i was like <i>"Oh dear, rich girl hating her privileged life...great"</i> but Shreffler made me eat my words and for the first time <u>I didn't mind whatsoever!</u><br /><br />Sora is an amazing character! She is not an amazingly strong girl, but she has spunk! The right amount of spunk that made you love her as the book progressed. <br /><br />Shreffler made me adore ALL the characters, the wolfies (Dorian and Burn) and Crash...a.k.a <i>Viper</i>! now <b>he</b> surprised me the most! This author made me grumble about this character for the first half of the book and absolutely LOVE him to death. <i>(No pun intended...no he doesn't die.)</i> <br /><br /><b>This book is action packed and so wonderful, i need the second book ASAP</b><br /><br />The Romance is not what you think! There's very little of it! however, don't let that discourage you! i think one of the character's is starting to figure out (at the end) that there is something there. SO I LOVE IT! because the second book is bound to have more of it...and i need more Viper in my life!<br /><br /><b>DID I MENTION THIS BOOK IS FOR FREE ON AMAZON!?</b><br /><br />GO GET IT PEOPLE! <br /><br /> </span>

  <span id="freeText11343777770176530511" style="display:none">So overall, I really enjoyed this- very promising for a series. Sora drove me up a wall in the beginning, but it's to be expected in YA that the heroine starts out naive (and sometimes downright stupid). If you want to predict her actions, you just have to think of the very last thing you would do ;-) HOWEVER, by the end she seemed liked she'd wizened up a bit, so I'll give her a fresh slate for the next book. I liked the vivid characters in this. Crash is complicated and intriguing, Dorian is mischievous and endearing and Burns is.... well just read the book already!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('q05ETI4gbGNV8/PIa30vSLCY6tykh5TyuA9EIt58ONAByipBut4eUhdFOuXm72IJOnXDYsvdqMMuTbAbr9J5kQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KbgbtNbuXpi+6vTJfKOGNzIBxt8Mp2JZoHh2dGUPq7eDPHW54hAsqfxcPeTxMct2uOzvYWP9Xmg2OoJNFKHq9g==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer12231066290225574960">T. L. Shreffler lives in Los Angeles, CA. She loves diversity, travel, and experiencing different cultures; she tries to evoke that same sense of unfamiliar wonder in her readers. She holds a BA in Eloquence (English) and her poetry has been published consecutively in <i>Eclipse: A Literary Journal</i> and <i>The Northridge Review</i>. She is author of <i>The Cat's Eye Chronicles</i> (YA/Epic Fantasy), The Dragon Pear</span>
  <span id="freeText12231066290225574960" style="display:none">T. L. Shreffler lives in Los Angeles, CA. She loves diversity, travel, and experiencing different cultures; she tries to evoke that same sense of unfamiliar wonder in her readers. She holds a BA in Eloquence (English) and her poetry has been published consecutively in <i>Eclipse: A Literary Journal</i> and <i>The Northridge Review</i>. She is author of <i>The Cat's Eye Chronicles</i> (YA/Epic Fantasy), The Dragon Pearl Series (YA/Epic Fantasy) and <i>The Wolves of Black River</i> (PN Romance.)</span>
